## internal/web/handlers.go

```go
package web

import (
	"bufio"
	"context"
	"encoding/json"
	"fmt"
	"html/template"
	"io"
	"log"
	"net/http"
	"os"
	"os/exec"
	"path/filepath"
	"strconv"
	"strings"
	"syscall"
	"time"

	"github.com/yuanguangshan/knowly/internal/ai"
	"github.com/yuanguangshan/knowly/internal/config"
	"github.com/yuanguangshan/knowly/internal/history"
	"github.com/yuanguangshan/knowly/internal/publisher"
	"github.com/yuanguangshan/knowly/internal/ssh"
)

// serveIndex 返回前端页面
func (s *Server) serveIndex(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
	if r.URL.Path != "/" {
		http.NotFound(w, r)
		return
	}
	w.Header().Set("Content-Type", "text/html; charset=utf-8")
	w.Header().Set("Cache-Control", "no-cache, no-store, must-revalidate")
	tmpl, err := template.New("index").Parse(string(indexHTML))
	if err != nil {
		http.Error(w, "template error", http.StatusInternalServerError)
		return
	}
	tmpl.Execute(w, map[string]interface{}{
		"RefreshSec":    s.cfg.Web.RefreshSec,
		"LogRefreshSec": s.cfg.Web.LogRefreshSec,
	})
}

// jsonResp 写入 JSON 响应
func jsonResp(w http.ResponseWriter, data interface{}) {
	w.Header().Set("Content-Type", "application/json; charset=utf-8")
	json.NewEncoder(w).Encode(data)
}

// jsonError 写入 JSON 错误
func jsonError(w http.ResponseWriter, msg string, code int) {
	w.Header().Set("Content-Type", "application/json; charset=utf-8")
	w.WriteHeader(code)
	json.NewEncoder(w).Encode(map[string]string{"error": msg})
}

// parseLogLine 解析日志行
func parseLogLine(line string) map[string]string {
	result := map[string]string{"raw": line}

	if len(line) >= 19 && line[4] == '/' && line[7] == '/' && line[10] == ' ' {
		result["time"] = line[:19]
		rest := strings.TrimSpace(line[19:])
		for _, level := range []string{"INFO", "WARN", "ERROR", "DEBUG"} {
			prefix := "[" + level + "] "
			if strings.HasPrefix(rest, prefix) {
				result["level"] = level
				result["message"] = rest[len(prefix):]
				return result
			}
		}
		result["message"] = rest
	}
	return result
}

// handleLogs 读取日志文件
func (s *Server) handleLogs(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
	level := r.URL.Query().Get("level")
	limitStr := r.URL.Query().Get("limit")
	limit := 200
	if n, err := strconv.Atoi(limitStr); err == nil && n > 0 {
		limit = n
	}

	logPath := config.GetLogPath()
	f, err := os.Open(logPath)
	if err != nil {
		jsonError(w, "无法读取日志文件", http.StatusInternalServerError)
		return
	}
	defer f.Close()

	var lines []string
	scanner := bufio.NewScanner(f)
	buf := make([]byte, 0, 64*1024)
	scanner.Buffer(buf, 2*1024*1024)
	for scanner.Scan() {
		line := scanner.Text()
		if level != "" && level != "all" {
			if !strings.Contains(line, "["+level+"]") {
				continue
			}
		}
		lines = append(lines, line)
	}

	if len(lines) > limit {
		lines = lines[len(lines)-limit:]
	}

	// 合并多行日志：非时间戳开头的行追加到上一条
	merged := make([]string, 0, len(lines))
	for _, line := range lines {
		if len(line) >= 19 && line[4] == '/' && line[7] == '/' && line[10] == ' ' {
			merged = append(merged, line)
		} else if len(merged) > 0 {
			merged[len(merged)-1] += "\n" + line
		}
	}

	result := make([]map[string]string, 0, len(merged))
	for _, line := range merged {
		result = append(result, parseLogLine(line))
	}

	jsonResp(w, result)
}

// handleLogStream SSE 实时日志流
func (s *Server) handleLogStream(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
	flusher, ok := w.(http.Flusher)
	if !ok {
		jsonError(w, "不支持 SSE", http.StatusInternalServerError)
		return
	}

	w.Header().Set("Content-Type", "text/event-stream")
	w.Header().Set("Cache-Control", "no-cache")
	w.Header().Set("Connection", "keep-alive")

	logPath := config.GetLogPath()

	// Start from current end of file, don't send historical logs
	// (frontend loads history separately via /api/logs)
	var offset int64
	if info, err := os.Stat(logPath); err == nil {
		offset = info.Size()
	}

	ctx := r.Context()
	ticker := time.NewTicker(1 * time.Second)
	defer ticker.Stop()

	for {
		select {
		case <-ctx.Done():
			return
		case <-ticker.C:
			f, err := os.Open(logPath)
			if err != nil {
				continue
			}

			if info, err := f.Stat(); err == nil {
				if info.Size() < offset {
					offset = 0
				}
			}

			f.Seek(offset, io.SeekStart)
			scanner := bufio.NewScanner(f)
			var pending string
			for scanner.Scan() {
				line := scanner.Text()
				if line == "" {
					continue
				}
				if len(line) >= 19 && line[4] == '/' && line[7] == '/' && line[10] == ' ' {
					if pending != "" {
						data, _ := json.Marshal(parseLogLine(pending))
						fmt.Fprintf(w, "data: %s\n\n", data)
						flusher.Flush()
					}
					pending = line
				} else if pending != "" {
					pending += "\n" + line
				}
			}
			if pending != "" {
				data, _ := json.Marshal(parseLogLine(pending))
				fmt.Fprintf(w, "data: %s\n\n", data)
				flusher.Flush()
			}

			if newOffset, err := f.Seek(0, io.SeekCurrent); err == nil {
				offset = newOffset
			}
			f.Close()
		}
	}
}

// handleArchiveList 列出归档目录
func (s *Server) handleArchiveList(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
	relPath := r.URL.Query().Get("path")
	fullPath := filepath.Join(s.cfg.SSH.BasePath, relPath)

	entries, err := s.sshClient.ListDir(fullPath)
	if err != nil {
		jsonError(w, fmt.Sprintf("无法列出目录: %v", err), http.StatusServiceUnavailable)
		return
	}

	jsonResp(w, entries)
}


// handleArchiveToday 一次性返回归档初始化数据（年/月/日列表 + 当日文件）
// 避免前端首次加载时串行 4 次 SSH 请求
func (s *Server) handleArchiveToday(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
	now := time.Now()
	year := fmt.Sprintf("%04d", now.Year())
	month := fmt.Sprintf("%02d", int(now.Month()))
	day := fmt.Sprintf("%02d", now.Day())

	type archiveTodayResp struct {
		Years   []ssh.DirEntry `json:"years"`
		Months  []ssh.DirEntry `json:"months"`
		Days    []ssh.DirEntry `json:"days"`
		Files   []ssh.DirEntry `json:"files"`
		Year    string         `json:"year"`
		Month   string         `json:"month"`
		Day     string         `json:"day"`
	}

	resp := archiveTodayResp{
		Year:  year,
		Month: month,
		Day:   day,
	}

	basePath := s.cfg.SSH.BasePath

	// 并行发起 SSH 请求
	type listResult struct {
		key     string
		entries []ssh.DirEntry
		err     error
	}
	ch := make(chan listResult, 4)

	listAsync := func(key, relPath string) {
		entries, err := s.sshClient.ListDir(filepath.Join(basePath, relPath))
		ch <- listResult{key: key, entries: entries, err: err}
	}

	go listAsync("years", "")
	go listAsync("months", year)
	go listAsync("days", year+"/"+month)
	go listAsync("files", year+"/"+month+"/"+day)

	for i := 0; i < 4; i++ {
		r := <-ch
		if r.err != nil {
			// 如果某级目录不存在（例如当天还没有归档），跳过
			log.Printf("[DEBUG] archiveToday: %s list failed: %v", r.key, r.err)
			continue
		}
		switch r.key {
		case "years":
			resp.Years = r.entries
		case "months":
			resp.Months = r.entries
		case "days":
			resp.Days = r.entries
		case "files":
			resp.Files = r.entries
		}
	}

	jsonResp(w, resp)
}

// handleArchiveFile 读取归档文件内容
func (s *Server) handleArchiveFile(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
	relPath := r.URL.Query().Get("path")
	if relPath == "" {
		jsonError(w, "缺少 path 参数", http.StatusBadRequest)
		return
	}

	fullPath := filepath.Join(s.cfg.SSH.BasePath, relPath)
	data, err := s.sshClient.ReadFile(fullPath)
	if err != nil {
		jsonError(w, fmt.Sprintf("无法读取文件: %v", err), http.StatusServiceUnavailable)
		return
	}

	ext := strings.ToLower(filepath.Ext(relPath))
	switch ext {
	case ".png":
		w.Header().Set("Content-Type", "image/png")
	case ".jpg", ".jpeg":
		w.Header().Set("Content-Type", "image/jpeg")
	case ".gif":
		w.Header().Set("Content-Type", "image/gif")
	case ".md", ".txt":
		w.Header().Set("Content-Type", "text/plain; charset=utf-8")
	default:
		w.Header().Set("Content-Type", "application/octet-stream")
	}

	w.Write(data)
}

// handleArchiveDownload 下载归档文件
func (s *Server) handleArchiveDownload(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
	relPath := r.URL.Query().Get("path")
	if relPath == "" {
		jsonError(w, "缺少 path 参数", http.StatusBadRequest)
		return
	}

	fullPath := filepath.Join(s.cfg.SSH.BasePath, relPath)
	data, err := s.sshClient.ReadFile(fullPath)
	if err != nil {
		jsonError(w, fmt.Sprintf("无法读取文件: %v", err), http.StatusServiceUnavailable)
		return
	}

	fileName := filepath.Base(relPath)
	w.Header().Set("Content-Disposition", "attachment; filename=\""+fileName+"\"")

	ext := strings.ToLower(filepath.Ext(relPath))
	switch ext {
	case ".png":
		w.Header().Set("Content-Type", "image/png")
	case ".md":
		w.Header().Set("Content-Type", "text/markdown; charset=utf-8")
	default:
		w.Header().Set("Content-Type", "application/octet-stream")
	}

	w.Write(data)
}

// handleHistory 读取本地历史记录
func (s *Server) handleHistory(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
	limitStr := r.URL.Query().Get("limit")
	typeFilter := r.URL.Query().Get("type")
	tagFilter := r.URL.Query().Get("tag")
	afterStr := r.URL.Query().Get("after")
	limit := 50
	if n, err := strconv.Atoi(limitStr); err == nil && n > 0 {
		limit = n
	}

	var entries []history.Entry
	var err error

	if afterStr != "" {
		// 分页：加载指定时间戳之前的条目
		afterTime, parseErr := time.Parse("2006-01-02 15:04:05", afterStr)
		if parseErr != nil {
			jsonError(w, "无效的 after 参数格式", http.StatusBadRequest)
			return
		}
		entries, err = s.histStore.RecentAfter(afterTime, limit)
	} else {
		entries, err = s.histStore.Recent(limit)
	}

	if err != nil {
		jsonError(w, fmt.Sprintf("无法读取历史: %v", err), http.StatusInternalServerError)
		return
	}

	type histEntry struct {
		ID        string   `json:"id"`
		Content   string   `json:"content"`
		Type      string   `json:"type"`
		Timestamp string   `json:"timestamp"`
		NASPath   string   `json:"nas_path"`
		Tags      []string `json:"tags"`
	}

	var result []histEntry
	for _, e := range entries {
		if typeFilter != "" && typeFilter != "all" && e.Type != typeFilter {
			continue
		}
		if tagFilter != "" {
			found := false
			for _, t := range e.Tags {
				if t == tagFilter {
					found = true
					break
				}
			}
			if !found {
				continue
			}
		}
		result = append(result, histEntry{
			ID:        e.ID,
			Content:   e.Content,
			Type:      e.Type,
			Timestamp: e.Timestamp.Format("2006-01-02 15:04:05"),
			NASPath:   e.NASPath,
			Tags:      e.Tags,
		})
	}

	jsonResp(w, result)
}

// handleTags 返回所有标签及计数
func (s *Server) handleTags(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
	tags, err := s.histStore.AllTags()
	if err != nil {
		jsonError(w, fmt.Sprintf("获取标签失败: %v", err), http.StatusInternalServerError)
		return
	}
	if tags == nil {
		tags = []history.TagCount{}
	}
	jsonResp(w, tags)
}

// handleStatus 返回守护进程状态
func (s *Server) handleStatus(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
	status := map[string]interface{}{
		"ssh": map[string]string{
			"host":      s.cfg.SSH.Host,
			"user":      s.cfg.SSH.User,
			"port":      s.cfg.SSH.Port,
			"base_path": s.cfg.SSH.BasePath,
		},
	}

	pidPath := config.GetPidPath()
	if data, err := os.ReadFile(pidPath); err == nil {
		pid, err := strconv.Atoi(strings.TrimSpace(string(data)))
		if err == nil {
			if proc, err := os.FindProcess(pid); err == nil && proc != nil {
				status["daemon_running"] = true
			}
		}
	}

	histFile := filepath.Join(config.GetConfigDir(), "history.jsonl")
	if f, err := os.Open(histFile); err == nil {
		scanner := bufio.NewScanner(f)
		scanner.Buffer(make([]byte, 0, 1024*1024), 10*1024*1024) // 10MB max line
		count := 0
		for scanner.Scan() {
			count++
		}
		f.Close()
		status["total_syncs"] = count
	}

	status["ssh_connected"] = s.sshClient != nil
	status["start_time"] = s.startTime.Format("2006-01-02 15:04:05")
	status["uptime"] = int64(time.Since(s.startTime).Seconds())
	status["pid"] = os.Getpid()

	// 读取版本号
	sourceDir := findProjectRoot()
	if sourceDir != "" {
		if pkgData, err := os.ReadFile(filepath.Join(sourceDir, "package.json")); err == nil {
			var pkg struct {
				Version string `json:"version"`
			}
			if json.Unmarshal(pkgData, &pkg) == nil {
				status["version"] = pkg.Version
			}
		}
	}

	// 发布渠道配置状态
	status["publishers"] = map[string]map[string]bool{
		"blog":    {"enabled": s.cfg.Blog.Enabled},
		"podcast": {"enabled": s.cfg.Podcast.Enabled},
		"ima":     {"enabled": s.cfg.IMA.Enabled && s.cfg.IMA.ClientID != "" && s.cfg.IMA.APIKey != ""},
		"kindle":  {"enabled": s.cfg.Kindle.Enabled && s.cfg.Kindle.SenderEmail != "" && s.cfg.Kindle.SenderPassword != ""},
	}

	jsonResp(w, status)
}

// handleRestart 重启 knowly daemon 进程
func (s *Server) handleRestart(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
	if r.Method != http.MethodPost {
		jsonError(w, "Method not allowed", http.StatusMethodNotAllowed)
		return
	}

	// 读取 daemon PID
	pidPath := config.GetPidPath()
	data, err := os.ReadFile(pidPath)
	if err != nil {
		jsonError(w, "守护进程未运行", http.StatusServiceUnavailable)
		return
	}
	pid, err := strconv.Atoi(strings.TrimSpace(string(data)))
	if err != nil {
		jsonError(w, "无效的 PID 文件", http.StatusInternalServerError)
		return
	}

	// 获取可执行文件路径
	exePath, err := os.Executable()
	if err != nil {
		jsonError(w, fmt.Sprintf("获取可执行文件路径失败: %v", err), http.StatusInternalServerError)
		return
	}

	jsonResp(w, map[string]string{"status": "restarting"})

	// 用 setsid 启动一个独立的 shell 脚本：先等旧进程退出，再启动新 daemon
	// 这样即使当前进程被 SIGTERM 杀掉，重启脚本仍会继续运行
	script := fmt.Sprintf(
		"kill -TERM %d; timeout 10 sh -c 'while kill -0 %d 2>/dev/null; do sleep 0.2; done' || kill -9 %d 2>/dev/null; sleep 0.5; exec %s --daemon",
		pid, pid, pid, exePath,
	)
	restartCmd := exec.Command("/bin/sh", "-c", script)
	restartCmd.Stdin = nil
	restartCmd.Stdout = nil
	restartCmd.Stderr = nil
	restartCmd.SysProcAttr = &syscall.SysProcAttr{Setpgid: true}
	if err := restartCmd.Start(); err != nil {
		log.Printf("[ERROR] restart: start restart script: %v", err)
	}
}

// handleUpdate 从源码编译并替换二进制文件，然后重启服务
func (s *Server) handleUpdate(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
	if r.Method != http.MethodPost {
		jsonError(w, "Method not allowed", http.StatusMethodNotAllowed)
		return
	}

	// 查找源码目录：从当前工作目录向上查找 go.mod
	sourceDir := findProjectRoot()
	if sourceDir == "" {
		jsonError(w, "找不到项目源码目录（未检测到 go.mod）", http.StatusInternalServerError)
		return
	}

	currentExe, err := os.Executable()
	if err != nil {
		jsonError(w, "获取当前可执行文件路径失败", http.StatusInternalServerError)
		return
	}
	tmpBinary := "knowly-update-tmp"

	// 设置 SSE
	w.Header().Set("Content-Type", "text/event-stream")
	w.Header().Set("Cache-Control", "no-cache")
	w.Header().Set("Connection", "keep-alive")
	flusher := w.(http.Flusher)

	sendEvent := func(step, msg string) {
		data, _ := json.Marshal(map[string]string{"step": step, "message": msg})
		fmt.Fprintf(w, "data: %s\n\n", data)
		flusher.Flush()
	}

	sendEvent("building", "编译中...")
	cmd := exec.Command("go", "build", "-o", tmpBinary, "./cmd/knowly")
	cmd.Dir = sourceDir
	output, err := cmd.CombinedOutput()
	if err != nil {
		sendEvent("error", fmt.Sprintf("编译失败: %s\n%s", err, string(output)))
		return
	}

	sendEvent("replacing", "替换二进制文件...")
	built := filepath.Join(sourceDir, tmpBinary)
	if err := os.Rename(built, currentExe); err != nil {
		sendEvent("error", fmt.Sprintf("替换失败: %v", err))
		return
	}

	// 提交并推送到远程
	sendEvent("pushing", "提交并推送到远程...")
	gitRun := func(name string, args ...string) (string, error) {
		cmd := exec.Command(name, args...)
		cmd.Dir = sourceDir
		out, err := cmd.CombinedOutput()
		return strings.TrimSpace(string(out)), err
	}
	gitRun("git", "add", "-A")
	if _, err := gitRun("git", "diff", "--cached", "--quiet"); err != nil {
		// 有变更，提交并推送
		if out, err := gitRun("git", "commit", "-m", "release"); err != nil && !strings.Contains(err.Error(), "nothing to commit") {
			sendEvent("pushing", "提交失败: "+out)
		} else if out, err := gitRun("git", "push"); err != nil {
			sendEvent("pushing", "推送失败: "+out)
		} else {
			sendEvent("pushing", "已提交并推送到远程")
		}
	} else {
		sendEvent("pushing", "无代码变更")
	}

	// 使用独立 shell 脚本重启（和 handleRestart 相同方式）
	// 脚本在独立进程组中运行，不受当前进程退出影响
	pidData, err := os.ReadFile(config.GetPidPath())
	if err != nil {
		sendEvent("error", fmt.Sprintf("读取 PID 文件失败: %v", err))
		return
	}
	pid, err := strconv.Atoi(strings.TrimSpace(string(pidData)))
	if err != nil {
		sendEvent("error", fmt.Sprintf("无效的 PID: %v", err))
		return
	}
	exePath, err := os.Executable()
	if err != nil {
		sendEvent("error", fmt.Sprintf("获取路径失败: %v", err))
		return
	}

	script := fmt.Sprintf(
		"sleep 1; kill -TERM %d; timeout 10 sh -c 'while kill -0 %d 2>/dev/null; do sleep 0.2; done' || kill -9 %d 2>/dev/null; sleep 0.5; exec %s --daemon",
		pid, pid, pid, exePath,
	)
	restartCmd := exec.Command("/bin/sh", "-c", script)
	restartCmd.Stdin = nil
	restartCmd.Stdout = nil
	restartCmd.Stderr = nil
	restartCmd.SysProcAttr = &syscall.SysProcAttr{Setpgid: true}
	if err := restartCmd.Start(); err != nil {
		sendEvent("error", fmt.Sprintf("启动重启脚本失败: %v", err))
		return
	}

	sendEvent("done", "更新完成，页面即将刷新")
}

// findProjectRoot 从当前目录向上查找包含 go.mod 的目录
func findProjectRoot() string {
	dir, err := os.Getwd()
	if err != nil {
		return ""
	}
	for i := 0; i < 20; i++ {
		if _, err := os.Stat(filepath.Join(dir, "go.mod")); err == nil {
			return dir
		}
		parent := filepath.Dir(dir)
		if parent == dir {
			break
		}
		dir = parent
	}
	return ""
}

// handleRelease 版本发布：git push → npm version minor → git push --tags
func (s *Server) handleRelease(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
	if r.Method != http.MethodPost {
		jsonError(w, "Method not allowed", http.StatusMethodNotAllowed)
		return
	}

	sourceDir := findProjectRoot()
	if sourceDir == "" {
		jsonError(w, "找不到项目源码目录", http.StatusInternalServerError)
		return
	}

	w.Header().Set("Content-Type", "text/event-stream")
	w.Header().Set("Cache-Control", "no-cache")
	w.Header().Set("Connection", "keep-alive")
	flusher := w.(http.Flusher)

	sendEvent := func(step, msg string) {
		data, _ := json.Marshal(map[string]string{"step": step, "message": msg})
		fmt.Fprintf(w, "data: %s\n\n", data)
		flusher.Flush()
	}

	run := func(name string, args ...string) (string, error) {
		cmd := exec.Command(name, args...)
		cmd.Dir = sourceDir
		out, err := cmd.CombinedOutput()
		return strings.TrimSpace(string(out)), err
	}

	// 1. git add & commit
	sendEvent("commit", "提交代码...")
	out, err := run("git", "add", "-A")
	if err != nil {
		sendEvent("error", "git add 失败: "+out)
		return
	}
	// 检查是否有变更
	out, _ = run("git", "diff", "--cached", "--quiet")
	// diff --cached --quiet 返回非0表示有变更
	out, err = run("git", "commit", "-m", "release")
	if err != nil && !strings.Contains(err.Error(), "nothing to commit") {
		// nothing to commit 也算正常
		sendEvent("commit", "无代码变更")
	} else {
		sendEvent("commit", "代码已提交")
	}

	// 2. git push
	sendEvent("push", "推送到远程...")
	if out, err = run("git", "push"); err != nil {
		sendEvent("error", "git push 失败: "+out)
		return
	}
	sendEvent("push", "推送完成")

	// 3. npm version minor
	sendEvent("version", "升级版本号...")
	if out, err = run("npm", "version", "minor"); err != nil {
		sendEvent("error", "npm version 失败: "+out)
		return
	}
	sendEvent("version", "版本: "+out)

	// 4. git push --tags
	sendEvent("tags", "推送标签...")
	if out, err = run("git", "push", "--tags"); err != nil {
		sendEvent("error", "git push --tags 失败: "+out)
		return
	}

	sendEvent("done", "发布完成")
}

// handlePublish 发布内容到 Blog/Podcast/IMA
func (s *Server) handlePublish(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
	if r.Method != http.MethodPost {
		jsonError(w, "Method not allowed", http.StatusMethodNotAllowed)
		return
	}

	var req struct {
		Content string   `json:"content"`
		Targets []string `json:"targets"`
	}
	if err := json.NewDecoder(r.Body).Decode(&req); err != nil {
		jsonError(w, "无效的请求体", http.StatusBadRequest)
		return
	}
	if req.Content == "" {
		jsonError(w, "内容不能为空", http.StatusBadRequest)
		return
	}

	// AI 生成标题和摘要
	content := req.Content
	if s.aiProcessor != nil {
		ctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(r.Context(), 30*time.Second)
		defer cancel()
		if result := s.aiProcessor.GenerateTitleAndSummary(ctx, content); result != nil {
			var header strings.Builder
			if result.Title != "" {
				header.WriteString("# " + result.Title + "\n\n")
			}
			if result.Summary != "" {
				header.WriteString("> " + result.Summary + "\n\n")
			}
			header.WriteString("---\n\n")
			content = header.String() + content
			log.Printf("[INFO] AI generated title and summary for publish")
		}
	}

	type publishResult struct {
		Target string `json:"target"`
		OK     bool   `json:"ok"`
		Error  string `json:"error,omitempty"`
	}
	var results []publishResult

	for _, target := range req.Targets {
		var err error
		switch target {
		case "blog":
			if s.cfg.Blog.APIURL == "" {
				err = fmt.Errorf("Blog API URL 未配置")
			} else {
				err = publisher.PublishBlog(s.cfg.Blog, content)
			}
		case "podcast":
			if s.cfg.Podcast.APIURL == "" {
				err = fmt.Errorf("Podcast API URL 未配置")
			} else {
				err = publisher.PublishPodcast(s.cfg.Podcast, content)
			}
		case "ima":
			if s.cfg.IMA.APIURL == "" || s.cfg.IMA.ClientID == "" || s.cfg.IMA.APIKey == "" {
				err = fmt.Errorf("IMA 配置不完整（需要 APIURL、ClientID、APIKey）")
			} else {
				err = publisher.PublishIMA(s.cfg.IMA, content)
			}
		case "kindle":
			if s.cfg.Kindle.KindleEmail == "" || s.cfg.Kindle.SenderEmail == "" || s.cfg.Kindle.SenderPassword == "" {
				err = fmt.Errorf("Kindle 配置不完整（需要 KindleEmail、SenderEmail、SenderPassword）")
			} else {
				err = publisher.PublishKindle(s.cfg.Kindle, content)
			}
		default:
			results = append(results, publishResult{Target: target, Error: "未知目标"})
			continue
		}
		if err != nil {
			results = append(results, publishResult{Target: target, OK: false, Error: err.Error()})
		} else {
			results = append(results, publishResult{Target: target, OK: true})
		}
	}

	jsonResp(w, results)
}

// handleTagAndPublish 添加标签并发布内容
// 注意：此接口不受全局 enabled 配置限制，允许手动触发发布
func (s *Server) handleTagAndPublish(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
	if r.Method != http.MethodPost {
		jsonError(w, "Method not allowed", http.StatusMethodNotAllowed)
		return
	}

	var req struct {
		ID     string `json:"id"`
		Tag    string `json:"tag"`
		Target string `json:"target"`
	}
	if err := json.NewDecoder(r.Body).Decode(&req); err != nil {
		jsonError(w, "无效的请求体", http.StatusBadRequest)
		return
	}
	if req.ID == "" || req.Tag == "" || req.Target == "" {
		jsonError(w, "缺少必要参数", http.StatusBadRequest)
		return
	}

	// 验证目标是否有效
	validTargets := map[string]bool{
		"ima":     true,
		"blog":    true,
		"kindle":  true,
		"podcast": true,
	}
	if !validTargets[req.Target] {
		jsonError(w, "无效的发布目标", http.StatusBadRequest)
		return
	}

	// 获取历史条目
	entry, err := s.histStore.GetByID(req.ID)
	if err != nil {
		jsonError(w, fmt.Sprintf("找不到条目: %v", err), http.StatusNotFound)
		return
	}

	// 添加标签（先添加标签，即使发布失败也保留标签）
	if err := s.histStore.UpdateTags(req.ID, []string{req.Tag}); err != nil {
		jsonError(w, fmt.Sprintf("添加标签失败: %v", err), http.StatusInternalServerError)
		return
	}

	// 获取完整内容
	content := entry.Content

	// 如果历史记录中只有预览内容，从 NAS 读取完整内容
	if entry.NASPath != "" && s.sshClient != nil {
		// NASPath 已经是完整绝对路径，直接读取
		data, err := s.sshClient.ReadFile(entry.NASPath)
		if err != nil {
			// NAS 读取失败，使用预览内容
			log.Printf("[WARN] Failed to read NAS file %s: %v, using preview content", entry.NASPath, err)
		} else {
			content = string(data)
		}
	}

	// 如果仍然没有内容，返回错误
	if content == "" {
		jsonError(w, "内容为空，无法发布", http.StatusBadRequest)
		return
	}

	// 优先使用同步时预生成的标题/摘要，避免重复 AI 调用
	var aiTitle, aiSummary string
	if entry.PublishTitle != "" {
		aiTitle = entry.PublishTitle
		aiSummary = entry.PublishSummary
		log.Printf("[INFO] Using cached publish title for %s", req.ID)
	} else if s.aiProcessor != nil {
		// 回退：旧数据没有预生成标题时才调 AI
		ctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(r.Context(), 30*time.Second)
		defer cancel()

		var result *ai.TitleAndSummary = s.aiProcessor.GenerateTitleAndSummary(ctx, content)
		if result != nil {
			aiTitle = result.Title
			aiSummary = result.Summary
			log.Printf("[INFO] AI generated title and summary for %s", req.ID)
		} else {
			log.Printf("[WARN] AI title generation failed for %s, using original content", req.ID)
		}
	}

	// 如果 AI 生成了标题和摘要，将它们添加到内容前面
	if aiTitle != "" || aiSummary != "" {
		var header strings.Builder
		if aiTitle != "" {
			header.WriteString("# " + aiTitle + "\n\n")
		}
		if aiSummary != "" {
			header.WriteString("> " + aiSummary + "\n\n")
		}
		header.WriteString("---\n\n")
		content = header.String() + content
	}

	// 发布内容（不受 enabled 配置限制）
	var publishErr error

	switch req.Target {
	case "blog":
		// 检查必要配置
		if s.cfg.Blog.APIURL == "" {
			publishErr = fmt.Errorf("Blog API URL 未配置")
		} else {
			publishErr = publisher.PublishBlog(s.cfg.Blog, content)
		}
	case "podcast":
		// 检查必要配置
		if s.cfg.Podcast.APIURL == "" {
			publishErr = fmt.Errorf("Podcast API URL 未配置")
		} else {
			publishErr = publisher.PublishPodcast(s.cfg.Podcast, content)
		}
	case "ima":
		// 检查必要配置
		if s.cfg.IMA.APIURL == "" || s.cfg.IMA.ClientID == "" || s.cfg.IMA.APIKey == "" {
			publishErr = fmt.Errorf("IMA 配置不完整（需要 APIURL、ClientID、APIKey）")
		} else {
			publishErr = publisher.PublishIMA(s.cfg.IMA, content)
		}
	case "kindle":
		// 检查必要配置
		if s.cfg.Kindle.KindleEmail == "" || s.cfg.Kindle.SenderEmail == "" || s.cfg.Kindle.SenderPassword == "" {
			publishErr = fmt.Errorf("Kindle 配置不完整（需要 KindleEmail、SenderEmail、SenderPassword）")
		} else {
			publishErr = publisher.PublishKindle(s.cfg.Kindle, content)
		}
	}

	result := map[string]interface{}{
		"tag_added": true,
		"target":    req.Target,
	}

	if publishErr != nil {
		result["published"] = false
		result["error"] = publishErr.Error()
	} else {
		result["published"] = true
	}

	jsonResp(w, result)
}

// handleStats 返回统计数据
func (s *Server) handleStats(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
	stats, err := s.histStore.Stats()
	if err != nil {
		jsonError(w, fmt.Sprintf("获取统计失败: %v", err), http.StatusInternalServerError)
		return
	}
	jsonResp(w, stats)
}

// handleSearch 全文搜索归档内容
func (s *Server) handleSearch(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
	keyword := r.URL.Query().Get("q")
	if keyword == "" {
		jsonError(w, "缺少搜索关键词", http.StatusBadRequest)
		return
	}
	limitStr := r.URL.Query().Get("limit")
	limit := 50
	if n, err := strconv.Atoi(limitStr); err == nil && n > 0 {
		limit = n
	}

	results, err := s.sshClient.Search(keyword, limit)
	if err != nil {
		jsonError(w, fmt.Sprintf("搜索失败: %v", err), http.StatusServiceUnavailable)
		return
	}
	if results == nil {
		results = []ssh.SearchResult{}
	}
	jsonResp(w, results)
}

// handleAIConfig 处理 AI 配置的读取和更新（GET/PUT）
func (s *Server) handleAIConfig(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
	switch r.Method {
	case http.MethodGet:
		s.handleGetAIConfig(w, r)
	case http.MethodPut:
		s.handleUpdateAIConfig(w, r)
	default:
		jsonError(w, "Method not allowed", http.StatusMethodNotAllowed)
	}
}

// handleGetAIConfig 返回当前 AI 配置（API Key 脱敏）
func (s *Server) handleGetAIConfig(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
	ai := s.cfg.AI

	// 构建 presets 列表
	presets := make(map[string]config.AIPresetOption)
	for k, v := range config.AIPresets {
		presets[k] = v
	}

	// 构建 prompt templates
	templates := make(map[string]string)
	for k, v := range config.AIPromptTemplates {
		templates[k] = v
	}

	// 脱敏 API Key
	masked := ai
	if len(masked.APIKey) > 4 {
		masked.APIKey = "****" + masked.APIKey[len(masked.APIKey)-4:]
	} else if masked.APIKey != "" {
		masked.APIKey = "****"
	}

	jsonResp(w, map[string]interface{}{
		"config":           masked,
		"presets":          presets,
		"prompt_templates": templates,
	})
}

// handleUpdateAIConfig 更新 AI 配置
func (s *Server) handleUpdateAIConfig(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
	var newCfg config.AIConfig
	if err := json.NewDecoder(r.Body).Decode(&newCfg); err != nil {
		jsonError(w, "无效的请求体", http.StatusBadRequest)
		return
	}

	// 预设解析：填充 endpoint 和 model
	if newCfg.Preset != "" && newCfg.Preset != "custom" {
		if p, ok := config.AIPresets[newCfg.Preset]; ok {
			if newCfg.Endpoint == "" {
				newCfg.Endpoint = p.Endpoint
			}
			if newCfg.Model == "" {
				newCfg.Model = p.Model
			}
		}
	}

	// 验证
	if newCfg.Enabled && newCfg.Endpoint == "" {
		jsonError(w, "启用 AI 时 endpoint 不能为空", http.StatusBadRequest)
		return
	}

	// 保留原有 API Key（如果传来的是脱敏值或空值）
	if newCfg.APIKey == "" || strings.HasPrefix(newCfg.APIKey, "****") {
		newCfg.APIKey = s.cfg.AI.APIKey
	}

	// 补全默认值
	if newCfg.MinContentLen == 0 {
		newCfg.MinContentLen = 100
	}
	if newCfg.MaxContentLen == 0 {
		newCfg.MaxContentLen = 10000
	}
	if newCfg.Timeout == 0 {
		newCfg.Timeout = 60
	}

	// 更新内存中的配置
	s.cfg.AI = newCfg

	// 持久化到磁盘
	if err := config.Save(s.cfg); err != nil {
		jsonError(w, fmt.Sprintf("保存配置失败: %v", err), http.StatusInternalServerError)
		return
	}

	promptMode := newCfg.PromptTemplate
	if promptMode == "" {
		if newCfg.Prompt == "" {
			promptMode = "默认"
		} else {
			promptMode = "自定义"
		}
	}
	log.Printf("[INFO] AI config updated (preset: %s, model: %s, endpoint: %s, prompt: %s)", newCfg.Preset, newCfg.Model, newCfg.Endpoint, promptMode)
	jsonResp(w, map[string]string{"status": "saved"})
}

// handleConfig 处理完整配置的读取和更新（GET/PUT）
func (s *Server) handleConfig(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
	switch r.Method {
	case http.MethodGet:
		s.handleGetConfig(w, r)
	case http.MethodPut:
		s.handleUpdateConfig(w, r)
	default:
		jsonError(w, "Method not allowed", http.StatusMethodNotAllowed)
	}
}

// maskField 脱敏字段：保留末4位
func maskField(val string) string {
	if len(val) > 4 {
		return "****" + val[len(val)-4:]
	} else if val != "" {
		return "****"
	}
	return ""
}

// sensitiveFields 需要脱敏的字段列表
var sensitiveFields = map[string]bool{
	"api_key":         true,
	"secret":          true,
	"auth":            true,
	"sender_password": true,
	"key_path":        false, // 路径不脱敏
}

// maskConfig 返回脱敏后的配置 JSON
func maskConfig(cfg *config.Config) map[string]interface{} {
	data, _ := json.Marshal(cfg)
	var m map[string]interface{}
	json.Unmarshal(data, &m)

	maskSensitive(m)
	return m
}

// maskSensitive 递归脱敏 map 中的敏感字段
func maskSensitive(m map[string]interface{}) {
	sensitive := map[string]bool{
		"api_key": true, "secret": true, "auth": true,
		"sender_password": true,
	}
	for k, v := range m {
		if sensitive[k] {
			if s, ok := v.(string); ok && s != "" {
				m[k] = maskField(s)
			}
		} else if nested, ok := v.(map[string]interface{}); ok {
			maskSensitive(nested)
		}
	}
}

// handleGetConfig 返回完整配置（敏感字段脱敏）
func (s *Server) handleGetConfig(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
	masked := maskConfig(s.cfg)
	jsonResp(w, masked)
}

// handleUpdateConfig 更新完整配置
func (s *Server) handleUpdateConfig(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
	var newCfg config.Config
	if err := json.NewDecoder(r.Body).Decode(&newCfg); err != nil {
		jsonError(w, "无效的请求体", http.StatusBadRequest)
		return
	}

	// 保留脱敏字段的原值
	oldJSON, _ := json.Marshal(s.cfg)
	newJSON, _ := json.Marshal(newCfg)
	var oldMap, newMap map[string]interface{}
	json.Unmarshal(oldJSON, &oldMap)
	json.Unmarshal(newJSON, &newMap)
	preserveMasked(oldMap, newMap)

	// 反序列化回结构体
	mergedJSON, _ := json.Marshal(newMap)
	var merged config.Config
	json.Unmarshal(mergedJSON, &merged)

	// 展开路径
	merged.SSH.KeyPath = config.ExpandPath(merged.SSH.KeyPath)
	merged.SSH.BasePath = config.ExpandPath(merged.SSH.BasePath)

	// 更新内存中的配置
	*s.cfg = merged

	// 持久化到磁盘
	if err := config.Save(s.cfg); err != nil {
		jsonError(w, fmt.Sprintf("保存配置失败: %v", err), http.StatusInternalServerError)
		return
	}

	log.Printf("[INFO] Config updated via web UI")
	jsonResp(w, map[string]string{"status": "saved"})
}

// preserveMasked 保留被脱敏的字段原值
func preserveMasked(old, new map[string]interface{}) {
	sensitive := map[string]bool{
		"api_key": true, "secret": true, "auth": true, "sender_password": true,
	}
	for k, v := range new {
		if sensitive[k] {
			if s, ok := v.(string); ok && strings.HasPrefix(s, "****") {
				new[k] = old[k]
			} else if s == "" {
				new[k] = old[k]
			}
		} else if nested, ok := v.(map[string]interface{}); ok {
			if oldNested, ok := old[k].(map[string]interface{}); ok {
				preserveMasked(oldNested, nested)
			}
		}
	}
}
```

````html
function showMotto() {
  const today = new Date();
  let m;
  if (today.getMonth() === 5 && today.getDate() === 13) {
    m = ['今天不仅是 Knowly 的版本号，也是创造者的诞辰', '祝生日快乐'];
  } else {
    m = mottos[Math.floor(Math.random() * mottos.length)];
  }
  document.getElementById('mottoBar').innerHTML =
    '<span class="motto-icon">&#9733;</span>' +
    '<span class="motto-text">' + m[0] + '</span>' +
    '<span class="motto-author">\u2014 ' + m[1] + '</span>';
}

// === State ===
let currentTab = 'logs';
let currentLevel = 'all';
let currentHistoryType = 'all';
let currentTagFilter = '';
let historyLoading = false;
let historyHasMore = true;
const historyPageSize = 30;
let currentFilePath = '';
let currentFileContent = '';
let selectedFileItem = null;
let eventSource = null;

// === Tab ===
var autoRefreshTimer = null;

function stopAutoRefresh() {
  if (autoRefreshTimer) { clearInterval(autoRefreshTimer); autoRefreshTimer = null; }
}

function startAutoRefresh(tab) {
  stopAutoRefresh();
  if (!REFRESH_SEC || REFRESH_SEC <= 0) return;
  var fn = null;
  if (tab === 'archive') fn = function() { loadYears(); };
  else if (tab === 'history') fn = function() { loadTags(); loadHistory(); };
  else if (tab === 'stats') fn = loadStats;
  if (fn) autoRefreshTimer = setInterval(fn, REFRESH_SEC * 1000);
}

function switchTab(tab) {
  currentTab = tab;
  stopAutoRefresh();
  document.querySelectorAll('.sidebar-item').forEach(el => el.classList.remove('active'));
  document.querySelectorAll('.tab-panel').forEach(el => el.classList.remove('active'));
  document.getElementById('tab-' + tab).classList.add('active');
  document.getElementById('panel-' + tab).classList.add('active');

  if (tab === 'logs') connectLogStream();
  else if (eventSource) { eventSource.close(); eventSource = null; }
  if (tab === 'archive' && document.getElementById('selYear').options.length <= 1) loadYears();
  if (tab === 'history') { loadTags(); loadHistory(); }
  if (tab === 'stats') loadStats();
  if (tab === 'admin') { loadAdminStatus(); loadAllConfig(); }
  startAutoRefresh(tab);
}

// === API Helper ===
async function api(path, options) {
  const res = await fetch(path, options);
  if (!res.ok) throw new Error(res.statusText);
  return res.json();
}

// === Toast ===
function showToast(msg) {
  const t = document.getElementById('toast');
  t.textContent = msg;
  t.classList.add('show');
  setTimeout(() => t.classList.remove('show'), 2000);
}

// === Clipboard ===
function copyText(text) {
  if (navigator.clipboard && navigator.clipboard.writeText) {
    navigator.clipboard.writeText(text).then(() => showToast('已复制')).catch(() => fallbackCopy(text));
  } else {
    fallbackCopy(text);
  }
}
function fallbackCopy(text) {
  const ta = document.createElement('textarea');
  ta.value = text;
  ta.style.cssText = 'position:fixed;left:-9999px';
  document.body.appendChild(ta);
  ta.select();
  document.execCommand('copy');
  document.body.removeChild(ta);
  showToast('已复制');
}

// === Logs ===
async function loadLogs() {
  try {
    const lines = await api('/api/logs?level=' + currentLevel + '&limit=200');
    const container = document.getElementById('logContainer');
    container.innerHTML = '';
    lines.forEach(l => appendLogLine(l));
  } catch (e) { console.error(e); }
}

function appendLogLine(line) {
  const container = document.getElementById('logContainer');
  var key = (line.time || '') + '|' + (line.raw || line.message || '');
  if (container.firstChild && container.firstChild.dataset && container.firstChild.dataset.key === key) return;
  var next = container.firstChild;
  while (next && next.dataset && next.dataset.key === key) { next = next.nextElementSibling; }
  const div = document.createElement('div');
  var level = line.level || '';
  div.className = 'log-line level-' + (level || 'PLAIN');
  div.dataset.key = key;
  div.dataset.raw = line.raw || line.message || '';
  var levelBadge = level ? escHtml(level) : '<span style="opacity:0.3">·</span>';
  div.innerHTML =
    '<span class="log-time">' + escHtml((line.time || '').replace(/^\d{4}\//, '')) + '</span>' +
    '<span class="log-level">' + levelBadge + '</span>' +
    '<span class="log-msg">' + escHtml(line.message || line.raw || '') + '</span>';
  container.insertBefore(div, container.firstChild);
}

function filterLogs(level) {
  currentLevel = level;
  document.querySelectorAll('#panel-logs .toolbar .btn').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
  event.target.classList.add('active');
  loadLogs();
}

function connectLogStream() {
  if (eventSource) { eventSource.close(); }
  eventSource = new EventSource('/api/logs/stream');
  eventSource.onmessage = function(e) {
    const line = JSON.parse(e.data);
    appendLogLine(line);
  };
  eventSource.onerror = function() { eventSource.close(); eventSource = null; };
}

// === Archive ===
let archiveInitialized = false;

async function loadYears() {
  if (archiveInitialized) return;
  archiveInitialized = true;

  try {
    const data = await api('/api/archive/today');
    const selYear = document.getElementById('selYear');
    const selMonth = document.getElementById('selMonth');
    const selDay = document.getElementById('selDay');

    // 填充年份下拉
    selYear.innerHTML = '<option value="">年份</option>';
    (data.years || []).filter(e => e.is_dir).sort((a, b) => b.name.localeCompare(a.name)).forEach(e => {
      selYear.innerHTML += '<option value="' + e.name + '">' + e.name + ' 年</option>';
    });
    if (data.year && selYear.querySelector('option[value="' + data.year + '"]')) {
      selYear.value = data.year;
    }

    // 填充月份下拉
    selMonth.innerHTML = '<option value="">月份</option>';
    selMonth.disabled = true;
    (data.months || []).filter(e => e.is_dir).sort((a, b) => b.name.localeCompare(a.name)).forEach(e => {
      selMonth.innerHTML += '<option value="' + e.name + '">' + e.name + ' 月</option>';
    });
    if (data.month && selMonth.querySelector('option[value="' + data.month + '"]')) {
      selMonth.value = data.month;
      selMonth.disabled = false;
    }

    // 填充日期下拉
    selDay.innerHTML = '<option value="">日期</option>';
    selDay.disabled = true;
    (data.days || []).filter(e => e.is_dir).sort((a, b) => b.name.localeCompare(a.name)).forEach(e => {
      selDay.innerHTML += '<option value="' + e.name + '">' + e.name + ' 日</option>';
    });
    if (data.day && selDay.querySelector('option[value="' + data.day + '"]')) {
      selDay.value = data.day;
      selDay.disabled = false;
    }

    // 渲染当日文件列表
    renderFileList(data.files || [], data.year + '/' + data.month + '/' + data.day);
  } catch (e) {
    document.getElementById('fileList').innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state">无法连接到远程服务器</div>';
  }
}

async function loadMonths() {
  const year = document.getElementById('selYear').value;
  const selMonth = document.getElementById('selMonth');
  const selDay = document.getElementById('selDay');
  selMonth.innerHTML = '<option value="">月份</option>';
  selMonth.disabled = true;
  selDay.innerHTML = '<option value="">日期</option>';
  selDay.disabled = true;
  document.getElementById('fileList').innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state">请选择日期查看文件</div>';
  clearPreview();
  if (!year) return;
  try {
    const entries = await api('/api/archive/list?path=' + year);
    selMonth.disabled = false;
    entries.filter(e => e.is_dir).sort((a, b) => b.name.localeCompare(a.name)).forEach(e => {
      selMonth.innerHTML += '<option value="' + e.name + '">' + e.name + ' 月</option>';
    });
  } catch (e) {}
}

async function loadDays() {
  const year = document.getElementById('selYear').value;
  const month = document.getElementById('selMonth').value;
  const selDay = document.getElementById('selDay');
  selDay.innerHTML = '<option value="">日期</option>';
  selDay.disabled = true;
  document.getElementById('fileList').innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state">请选择日期查看文件</div>';
  clearPreview();
  if (!month) return;
  try {
    const entries = await api('/api/archive/list?path=' + year + '/' + month);
    selDay.disabled = false;
    entries.filter(e => e.is_dir).sort((a, b) => b.name.localeCompare(a.name)).forEach(e => {
      selDay.innerHTML += '<option value="' + e.name + '">' + e.name + ' 日</option>';
    });
  } catch (e) {}
}

function renderFileList(entries, path) {
  const list = document.getElementById('fileList');
  const files = entries.filter(e => !e.is_dir).sort((a, b) => b.name.localeCompare(a.name));
  if (files.length === 0) {
    list.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state">当日无文件</div>';
    return;
  }
  list.innerHTML = '';
  files.forEach(f => {
    const div = document.createElement('div');
    div.className = 'file-item';
    const isImg = f.name.endsWith('.png') || f.name.endsWith('.jpg');
    const icon = isImg ? '🖼' : '📄';
    const sizeStr = f.size > 1024 ? (f.size / 1024).toFixed(1) + ' KB' : f.size + ' B';
    div.innerHTML =
      '<span class="file-icon">' + icon + '</span>' +
      '<div class="file-info">' +
        '<div class="file-name">' + escHtml(f.name) + '</div>' +
        '<div class="file-meta">' + escHtml(f.mod_time) + ' · ' + sizeStr + '</div>' +
      '</div>';
    div.onclick = function() { previewFile(path + '/' + f.name, f.name, div); };
    list.appendChild(div);
  });
}

async function loadFiles() {
  const year = document.getElementById('selYear').value;
  const month = document.getElementById('selMonth').value;
  const day = document.getElementById('selDay').value;
  const list = document.getElementById('fileList');
  clearPreview();

  if (!day) { list.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state">请选择日期</div>'; return; }

  try {
    const path = year + '/' + month + '/' + day;
    const entries = await api('/api/archive/list?path=' + path);
    renderFileList(entries, path);
  } catch (e) { list.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state">加载失败</div>'; }
}

async function previewFile(path, name, itemEl) {
  if (selectedFileItem) selectedFileItem.classList.remove('selected');
  if (itemEl) itemEl.classList.add('selected');
  selectedFileItem = itemEl;
  currentFilePath = path;

  const preview = document.getElementById('previewContent');
  const toolbar = document.getElementById('previewToolbar');
  const title = document.getElementById('previewTitle');
  toolbar.style.display = 'flex';
  title.textContent = name;

  const isImg = name.endsWith('.png') || name.endsWith('.jpg') || name.endsWith('.jpeg');

  if (isImg) {
    preview.innerHTML = '<img src="/api/archive/file?path=' + encodeURIComponent(path) + '" style="max-width:100%">';
    currentFileContent = '';
    document.getElementById('publishDropdown').style.display = 'none';
  } else {
    try {
      const res = await fetch('/api/archive/file?path=' + encodeURIComponent(path));
      const text = await res.text();
      currentFileContent = text;
      // Strip YAML frontmatter
      let content = text;
      if (content.startsWith('---')) {
        const end = content.indexOf('---', 3);
        if (end > 0) content = content.substring(end + 3).trim();
      }
      preview.innerHTML = '<div class="md-body">' + renderMarkdown(content) + '</div>';
      document.getElementById('publishDropdown').style.display = 'inline-block';
    } catch (e) {
      preview.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state">加载失败</div></div>';
      document.getElementById('publishDropdown').style.display = 'none';    }
  }
}

function clearPreview() {
  document.getElementById('previewToolbar').style.display = 'none';
  document.getElementById('publishDropdown').style.display = 'none';
  document.getElementById('previewContent').innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state">选择文件预览</div>';
  currentFilePath = '';
  currentFileContent = '';
  if (selectedFileItem) { selectedFileItem.classList.remove('selected'); selectedFileItem = null; }
}

function copyPreviewContent() {
  if (currentFileContent) copyText(currentFileContent);
  else showToast('无文本内容');
}

function downloadFile() {
  if (!currentFilePath) return;
  const a = document.createElement('a');
  a.href = '/api/archive/download?path=' + encodeURIComponent(currentFilePath);
  a.click();
}

// === Markdown Renderer ===
function renderMarkdown(text) {
  // Code blocks
  text = text.replace(/```(\w*)\n([\s\S]*?)```/g, function(m, lang, code) {
    return '<pre><code>' + escHtml(code.trim()) + '</code></pre>';
  });
  // Inline code
  text = text.replace(/`([^`]+)`/g, '<code>$1</code>');
  // Headings
  text = text.replace(/^### (.+)$/gm, '<h3>$1</h3>');
  text = text.replace(/^## (.+)$/gm, '<h2>$1</h2>');
  text = text.replace(/^# (.+)$/gm, '<h1>$1</h1>');
  // Bold
  text = text.replace(/\*\*(.+?)\*\*/g, '<strong>$1</strong>');
  // Italic
  text = text.replace(/\*(.+?)\*/g, '<em>$1</em>');
  // Links
  text = text.replace(/\[([^\]]+)\]\(([^)]+)\)/g, '<a href="$2" target="_blank">$1</a>');
  // Blockquote
  text = text.replace(/^> (.+)$/gm, '<blockquote>$1</blockquote>');
  // Unordered list
  text = text.replace(/^[*-] (.+)$/gm, '<li>$1</li>');
  text = text.replace(/(<li>.*<\/li>\n?)+/g, '<ul>$&</ul>');
  // Paragraphs: double newline
  text = text.replace(/\n\n+/g, '\n</p><p>\n');
  // Single newline within paragraph -> <br>
  text = text.replace(/\n/g, '<br>\n');
  // Wrap in paragraph
  text = '<p>' + text + '</p>';
  // Clean up empty paragraphs
  text = text.replace(/<p>\s*<\/p>/g, '');
  text = text.replace(/<p>\s*(<h[123]>)/g, '$1');
  text = text.replace(/(<\/h[123]>)\s*<\/p>/g, '$1');
  text = text.replace(/<p>\s*(<pre>)/g, '$1');
  text = text.replace(/(<\/pre>)\s*<\/p>/g, '$1');
  text = text.replace(/<p>\s*(<ul>)/g, '$1');
  text = text.replace(/(<\/ul>)\s*<\/p>/g, '$1');
  text = text.replace(/<p>\s*(<blockquote>)/g, '$1');
  text = text.replace(/(<\/blockquote>)\s*<\/p>/g, '$1');
  return text;
}

// === History ===
let tagsExpanded = false;
async function loadTags() {
  try {
    const tags = await api('/api/tags');
    const bar = document.getElementById('tagsBar');
    if (!tags.length) { bar.innerHTML = ''; return; }
    let html = '<span class="tag-item' + (currentTagFilter === '' ? ' active' : '') + '" data-tag="">全部</span>';

    // 如果标签数量大于3，默认折叠
    const showTags = tagsExpanded ? tags : tags.slice(0, 3);
    showTags.forEach(t => {
      html += '<span class="tag-item' + (currentTagFilter === t.tag ? ' active' : '') + '" data-tag="' + escHtml(t.tag) + '">' + escHtml(t.tag) + '<small>' + t.count + '</small></span>';
    });

    // 更新工具栏中的展开/折叠按钮
    const toggle = document.getElementById('tagsToggle');
    if (toggle) {
      if (tags.length > 3) {
        toggle.style.display = '';
        toggle.textContent = tagsExpanded ? '收起' : '展开更多';
      } else {
        toggle.style.display = 'none';
      }
    }

    bar.innerHTML = html;
  } catch (e) { console.error(e); }
}

function toggleTags(event) {
  event.stopPropagation();
  tagsExpanded = !tagsExpanded;
  loadTags();
}

function filterByTag(tag) {
  currentTagFilter = tag;
  loadTags();
  loadHistory();
}

async function loadHistory(append) {
  if (historyLoading) return;
  const list = document.getElementById('historyList');

  if (!append) {
    historyHasMore = true;
    list.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state">加载中...</div>';
  } else {
    if (!historyHasMore) return;
  }

  historyLoading = true;
  try {
    let url = '/api/history?limit=' + historyPageSize + '&type=' + currentHistoryType;
    if (currentTagFilter) url += '&tag=' + encodeURIComponent(currentTagFilter);

    // 分页：取最后一条的时间戳作为游标
    if (append) {
      const items = list.querySelectorAll('.history-item');
      const lastItem = items[items.length - 1];
      if (lastItem) {
        const ts = lastItem.querySelector('.history-time');
        if (ts && ts.textContent) {
          url += '&after=' + encodeURIComponent(ts.textContent.trim());
        }
      }
    }

    const entries = await api(url);

    if (entries.length < historyPageSize) {
      historyHasMore = false;
    }

    if (entries.length === 0 && !append) {
      list.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state">暂无历史记录</div>';
    } else if (entries.length > 0) {
      if (!append) list.innerHTML = '';
      entries.forEach(e => {
        const div = document.createElement('div');
        div.className = 'history-item';
        const typeLabel = e.type === 'text' ? '文本' : '图片';
        const lines = (e.content || '').split('\n').filter(l => l.trim());
        const preview = lines.slice(0, 3).join('\n') + (lines.length > 3 ? '\n...' : '');
        let tagsHtml = '';
        if (e.tags && e.tags.length) {
          tagsHtml = '<span class="history-tags">' + e.tags.map(t => '<span class="htag">#' + escHtml(t) + '</span>').join('') + '</span>';
        }
        div.innerHTML =
          '<div class="history-header">' +
            '<span class="history-time">' + escHtml(e.timestamp || '') + '</span>' +
            '<span class="history-type ' + e.type + '">' + typeLabel + '</span>' +
            '<div class="history-quick-actions">' +
              '<button class="quick-tag-btn" data-id="' + escHtml(e.id) + '" data-tag="Ima" data-target="ima" title="添加 Ima 标签并发布">+ Ima</button>' +
              '<button class="quick-tag-btn" data-id="' + escHtml(e.id) + '" data-tag="Blog" data-target="blog" title="添加 Blog 标签并发布">+ Blog</button>' +
              '<button class="quick-tag-btn" data-id="' + escHtml(e.id) + '" data-tag="Kindle" data-target="kindle" title="添加 Kindle 标签并发布">+ Kindle</button>' +
              '<button class="quick-tag-btn" data-id="' + escHtml(e.id) + '" data-tag="Podcast" data-target="podcast" title="添加 Podcast 标签并发布">+ Podcast</button>' +
            '</div>' +
          '</div>' +
          '<div class="history-preview">' + escHtml(preview) + '</div>' +
          tagsHtml;
        div.onclick = function(ev) {
          if (ev.target.classList.contains('quick-tag-btn')) return;
          toggleHistoryDetail(div, e);
        };
        list.appendChild(div);
      });
    }
  } catch (e) {
    if (!append) list.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state">加载失败</div>';
  } finally {
    historyLoading = false;
  }
}

// 历史列表无限滚动
document.getElementById('historyList').addEventListener('scroll', function() {
  if (historyLoading || !historyHasMore) return;
  const el = this;
  if (el.scrollTop + el.clientHeight >= el.scrollHeight - 100) {
    loadHistory(true);
  }
});

function toggleHistoryDetail(el, entry) {
  const existing = el.querySelector('.history-detail');
  if (existing) { existing.remove(); return; }

  const detail = document.createElement('div');
  detail.className = 'history-detail';
  detail.innerHTML = escHtml(entry.content || '') +
    '<span class="copy-btn btn" data-copy="' + escHtml(entry.content || '') + '"></span>';

  detail.querySelector('.copy-btn').addEventListener('click', function(e) {
    e.stopPropagation();
    copyText(this.dataset.copy || '');
  });
  el.appendChild(detail);
}

function filterHistory(type) {
  currentHistoryType = type;
  document.querySelectorAll('#panel-history .toolbar .btn').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
  event.target.classList.add('active');
  loadHistory();
}

// 快捷标签按钮点击处理（事件委托）
document.addEventListener('click', async function(e) {
  if (!e.target.classList.contains('quick-tag-btn')) return;

  e.stopPropagation();
  const btn = e.target;
  const id = btn.dataset.id;
  const tag = btn.dataset.tag;
  const target = btn.dataset.target;

  // 禁用按钮，防止重复点击
  btn.disabled = true;
  const originalText = btn.textContent;
  btn.textContent = '处理中...';

  try {
    const result = await api('/api/tag-and-publish', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({ id, tag, target })
    });

    if (result.published) {
      btn.textContent = '✓ 已发布';
      btn.classList.add('success');
      // 重新加载历史列表以显示更新的标签
      setTimeout(() => loadHistory(), 1000);
    } else {
      btn.textContent = '✗ 失败';
      btn.classList.add('error');
      console.error('发布失败:', result.error);
    }
  } catch (err) {
    btn.textContent = '✗ 失败';
    btn.classList.add('error');
    console.error('请求失败:', err);
  }

  // 3秒后恢复按钮状态
  setTimeout(() => {
    btn.disabled = false;
    btn.textContent = originalText;
    btn.classList.remove('success', 'error');
  }, 3000);
});

// === Stats ===
let publishersConfig = {};

async function loadStats() {
  try {
    const s = await api('/api/stats');
    document.getElementById('statsTotalSyncs').textContent = s.total_syncs;
    document.getElementById('statsTextCount').textContent = s.text_count;
    document.getElementById('statsImageCount').textContent = s.image_count;
    drawWeeklyChart(s.weekly_trend || []);
    drawTypeChart(s.text_count, s.image_count);
    drawDailyChart(s.daily_trend || []);
  } catch (e) { console.error(e); }
}

function drawWeeklyChart(data) {
  const canvas = document.getElementById('weeklyChart');
  const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
  const dpr = window.devicePixelRatio || 1;
  const rect = canvas.getBoundingClientRect();
  canvas.width = rect.width * dpr;
  canvas.height = 200 * dpr;
  ctx.scale(dpr, dpr);
  const W = rect.width, H = 200;
  ctx.clearRect(0, 0, W, H);

  if (!data.length) { ctx.fillStyle = '#8892a4'; ctx.font = '13px sans-serif'; ctx.fillText('暂无数据', W/2-30, H/2); return; }

  const pad = {top:20, right:20, bottom:30, left:40};
  const cw = W - pad.left - pad.right;
  const ch = H - pad.top - pad.bottom;
  const maxVal = Math.max(...data.map(d => d.count), 1);
  const barW = Math.max(cw / data.length * 0.6, 4);
  const gap = cw / data.length;

  // Y axis
  ctx.strokeStyle = '#2a2a4a'; ctx.lineWidth = 1;
  for (let i = 0; i <= 4; i++) {
    const y = pad.top + ch * (1 - i/4);
    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(pad.left, y); ctx.lineTo(W - pad.right, y); ctx.stroke();
    ctx.fillStyle = '#8892a4'; ctx.font = '11px sans-serif'; ctx.textAlign = 'right';
    ctx.fillText(Math.round(maxVal * i/4), pad.left - 6, y + 4);
  }

  data.forEach((d, i) => {
    const x = pad.left + gap * i + gap/2 - barW/2;
    const totalH = (d.count / maxVal) * ch;
    const textH = (d.text_count / maxVal) * ch;
    const imgH = (d.image_count / maxVal) * ch;
    const y = pad.top + ch - totalH;
    // Text bar (bottom)
    ctx.fillStyle = '#4fc3f7';
    ctx.fillRect(x, y + imgH, barW, textH);
    // Image bar (top)
    ctx.fillStyle = '#66bb6a';
    ctx.fillRect(x, y, barW, imgH);
    // Label
    ctx.fillStyle = '#8892a4'; ctx.font = '10px sans-serif'; ctx.textAlign = 'center';
    const label = d.label.split('-W')[1] || d.label;
    ctx.fillText('W' + label, pad.left + gap * i + gap/2, H - 8);
  });

  // Legend
  ctx.fillStyle = '#4fc3f7'; ctx.fillRect(W - 120, 6, 10, 10);
  ctx.fillStyle = '#8892a4'; ctx.font = '11px sans-serif'; ctx.textAlign = 'left';
  ctx.fillText('文本', W - 106, 15);
  ctx.fillStyle = '#66bb6a'; ctx.fillRect(W - 60, 6, 10, 10);
  ctx.fillStyle = '#8892a4'; ctx.fillText('图片', W - 46, 15);
}

function drawTypeChart(textCount, imageCount) {
  const canvas = document.getElementById('typeChart');
  const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
  const dpr = window.devicePixelRatio || 1;
  const rect = canvas.getBoundingClientRect();
  canvas.width = rect.width * dpr;
  canvas.height = 200 * dpr;
  ctx.scale(dpr, dpr);
  const W = rect.width, H = 200;
  ctx.clearRect(0, 0, W, H);

  const total = textCount + imageCount;
  if (total === 0) { ctx.fillStyle = '#8892a4'; ctx.font = '13px sans-serif'; ctx.fillText('暂无数据', W/2-30, H/2); return; }

  const cx = W / 2, cy = H / 2 - 5;
  const r = Math.min(cx, cy) - 30;
  const textAngle = (textCount / total) * Math.PI * 2;

  // Text slice
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.moveTo(cx, cy);
  ctx.arc(cx, cy, r, -Math.PI/2, -Math.PI/2 + textAngle);
  ctx.closePath();
  ctx.fillStyle = '#4fc3f7';
  ctx.fill();

  // Image slice
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.moveTo(cx, cy);
  ctx.arc(cx, cy, r, -Math.PI/2 + textAngle, -Math.PI/2 + Math.PI*2);
  ctx.closePath();
  ctx.fillStyle = '#66bb6a';
  ctx.fill();

  // Center hole (donut)
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.arc(cx, cy, r * 0.5, 0, Math.PI * 2);
  ctx.fillStyle = '#1f2b47';
  ctx.fill();

  // Labels
  ctx.font = '12px sans-serif'; ctx.textAlign = 'center';
  if (textCount > 0) {
    const tAngle = -Math.PI/2 + textAngle/2;
    const lx = cx + (r*0.75) * Math.cos(tAngle);
    const ly = cy + (r*0.75) * Math.sin(tAngle);
    ctx.fillStyle = '#fff'; ctx.fillText(Math.round(textCount/total*100)+'%', lx, ly+4);
  }
  if (imageCount > 0) {
    const iAngle = -Math.PI/2 + textAngle + (Math.PI*2 - textAngle)/2;
    const lx = cx + (r*0.75) * Math.cos(iAngle);
    const ly = cy + (r*0.75) * Math.sin(iAngle);
    ctx.fillStyle = '#fff'; ctx.fillText(Math.round(imageCount/total*100)+'%', lx, ly+4);
  }

  // Legend
  ctx.font = '12px sans-serif';
  ctx.fillStyle = '#4fc3f7'; ctx.fillRect(10, H-24, 10, 10);
  ctx.fillStyle = '#e6e6e6'; ctx.textAlign = 'left'; ctx.fillText('文本 ' + textCount, 24, H-15);
  ctx.fillStyle = '#66bb6a'; ctx.fillRect(W/2, H-24, 10, 10);
  ctx.fillStyle = '#e6e6e6'; ctx.fillText('图片 ' + imageCount, W/2+14, H-15);
}

function drawDailyChart(data) {
  const canvas = document.getElementById('dailyChart');
  const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
  const dpr = window.devicePixelRatio || 1;
  const rect = canvas.getBoundingClientRect();
  canvas.width = rect.width * dpr;
  canvas.height = 200 * dpr;
  ctx.scale(dpr, dpr);
  const W = rect.width, H = 200;
  ctx.clearRect(0, 0, W, H);

  if (!data.length) { ctx.fillStyle = '#8892a4'; ctx.font = '13px sans-serif'; ctx.fillText('暂无数据', W/2-30, H/2); return; }

  const pad = {top:20, right:20, bottom:30, left:40};
  const cw = W - pad.left - pad.right;
  const ch = H - pad.top - pad.bottom;
  const maxVal = Math.max(...data.map(d => d.count), 1);

  // Y axis
  ctx.strokeStyle = '#2a2a4a'; ctx.lineWidth = 1;
  for (let i = 0; i <= 4; i++) {
    const y = pad.top + ch * (1 - i/4);
    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(pad.left, y); ctx.lineTo(W - pad.right, y); ctx.stroke();
    ctx.fillStyle = '#8892a4'; ctx.font = '11px sans-serif'; ctx.textAlign = 'right';
    ctx.fillText(Math.round(maxVal * i/4), pad.left - 6, y + 4);
  }

  // Line
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.strokeStyle = '#4fc3f7';
  ctx.lineWidth = 2;
  ctx.lineJoin = 'round';
  const step = cw / (data.length - 1 || 1);
  data.forEach((d, i) => {
    const x = pad.left + step * i;
    const y = pad.top + ch - (d.count / maxVal) * ch;
    if (i === 0) ctx.moveTo(x, y); else ctx.lineTo(x, y);
  });
  ctx.stroke();

  // Fill area
  ctx.lineTo(pad.left + step * (data.length - 1), pad.top + ch);
  ctx.lineTo(pad.left, pad.top + ch);
  ctx.closePath();
  ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(79, 195, 247, 0.1)';
  ctx.fill();

  // Dots
  data.forEach((d, i) => {
    const x = pad.left + step * i;
    const y = pad.top + ch - (d.count / maxVal) * ch;
    if (d.count > 0) {
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(x, y, 3, 0, Math.PI*2);
      ctx.fillStyle = '#4fc3f7'; ctx.fill();
    }
  });

  // X labels (every 5 days)
  ctx.fillStyle = '#8892a4'; ctx.font = '10px sans-serif'; ctx.textAlign = 'center';
  data.forEach((d, i) => {
    if (i % 5 === 0 || i === data.length - 1) {
      const x = pad.left + step * i;
      ctx.fillText(d.date.substring(5), x, H - 8);
    }
  });
}

// === Search ===
let searchKeyword = '';

async function searchArchive() {
  const input = document.getElementById('searchInput');
  const keyword = input.value.trim();
  if (!keyword) { showToast('请输入搜索关键词'); return; }
  searchKeyword = keyword;

  const resultsEl = document.getElementById('searchResults');
  const fileListEl = document.getElementById('fileList');
  const breadcrumbEl = document.querySelector('.archive-breadcrumb');

  resultsEl.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state">搜索中...</div>';
  resultsEl.style.display = 'block';
  fileListEl.style.display = 'none';
  breadcrumbEl.style.display = 'none';

  try {
    const results = await api('/api/search?q=' + encodeURIComponent(keyword));
    if (!results.length) {
      resultsEl.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state">未找到匹配结果</div>';
      return;
    }
    resultsEl.innerHTML = '';
    results.forEach(r => {
      const div = document.createElement('div');
      div.className = 'search-result-item';
      const highlighted = highlightMatch(escHtml(r.content), keyword);
      div.innerHTML =
        '<div class="search-result-path">' + escHtml(r.path) + ' : ' + r.line + '</div>' +
        '<div class="search-result-content">' + highlighted + '</div>';
      div.onclick = function() { openSearchResult(r.path); };
      resultsEl.appendChild(div);
    });
  } catch (e) {
    resultsEl.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state">搜索失败</div>';
  }
}

function highlightMatch(text, keyword) {
  if (!keyword) return text;
  const re = new RegExp('(' + keyword.replace(/[.*+?^${}()|[\]\\]/g, '\\$&') + ')', 'gi');
  return text.replace(re, '<span class="search-highlight">$1</span>');
}

function openSearchResult(path) {
  // 从路径解析 年/月/日/文件名
  const parts = path.split('/');
  if (parts.length >= 4) {
    const year = parts[0], month = parts[1], day = parts[2], fileName = parts.slice(3).join('/');
    document.getElementById('selYear').value = year;
    document.getElementById('selMonth').innerHTML = '<option value="' + month + '">' + month + ' 月</option>';
    document.getElementById('selMonth').value = month;
    document.getElementById('selDay').innerHTML = '<option value="' + day + '">' + day + ' 日</option>';
    document.getElementById('selDay').value = day;
  }
  // 隐藏搜索结果，显示文件列表
  document.getElementById('searchResults').style.display = 'none';
  document.querySelector('.archive-breadcrumb').style.display = 'flex';
  document.getElementById('fileList').style.display = 'block';

  // 直接预览该文件
  const relPath = path;
  previewFile(relPath, parts[parts.length-1], null);
}

function clearSearch() {
  document.getElementById('searchResults').style.display = 'none';
  document.querySelector('.archive-breadcrumb').style.display = 'flex';
  document.getElementById('fileList').style.display = 'block';
}

// === Publish ===
function togglePublishMenu() {
  const menu = document.getElementById('publishMenu');
  menu.classList.toggle('open');
}

async function publishContent(target) {
  const menu = document.getElementById('publishMenu');
  const item = menu.querySelector('[data-target="'+target+'"]');
  menu.classList.remove('open');

  // Strip YAML frontmatter for publish
  let content = currentFileContent || '';
  if (content.startsWith('---')) {
    const end = content.indexOf('---', 3);
    if (end > 0) content = content.substring(end + 3).trim();
  }
  if (!content) { showToast('无内容可发布'); return; }

  showToast('正在发布到 ' + target + '...');

  try {
    const res = await fetch('/api/publish', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: {'Content-Type': 'application/json'},
      body: JSON.stringify({content: content, targets: [target]})
    });
    const results = await res.json();
    const r = results[0];
    if (r && r.ok) {
      showToast('已发布到 ' + target);
    } else {
      showToast('发布失败: ' + (r ? r.error : '未知错误'));
    }
  } catch (e) {
    showToast('发布请求失败');
  }
}

// Close publish menu on outside click
document.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
  const dropdown = document.getElementById('publishDropdown');
  if (dropdown && !dropdown.contains(e.target)) {
    document.getElementById('publishMenu').classList.remove('open');
  }
});

// === Status ===
let adminStatus = null;
let adminTimer = null;

async function loadStatus() {
  try {
    const s = await api('/api/status');
    adminStatus = s;
    const el = document.getElementById('headerStatus');
    const sshDot = s.ssh_connected ? '<span class="status-dot on"></span>' : '<span class="status-dot off"></span>';
    const daemonDot = s.daemon_running ? '<span class="status-dot on"></span>' : '<span class="status-dot off"></span>';
    el.innerHTML =
      '<span>' + daemonDot + '守护进程</span>' +
      '<span>' + sshDot + 'SSH</span>' +
      '<span>同步: ' + (s.total_syncs || 0) + '</span>';
    if (s.publishers) publishersConfig = s.publishers;
  } catch (e) {}
}

// === Admin ===
async function loadAdminStatus() {
  try {
    const s = await api('/api/status');
    s._fetchedAt = Date.now();
    adminStatus = s;
    document.getElementById('adminPid').textContent = s.pid || '-';
    document.getElementById('adminVersion').textContent = s.version || '-';
    document.getElementById('adminStartTime').textContent = s.start_time || '-';
    document.getElementById('adminSyncs').textContent = s.total_syncs || 0;
    updateUptime();
    if (adminTimer) clearInterval(adminTimer);
    adminTimer = setInterval(updateUptime, 1000);
  } catch (e) {}
}

function toggleCard(header) {
  header.parentElement.classList.toggle('collapsed');
}

async function loadAllConfig() {
  try {
    const [config, aiData] = await Promise.all([api('/api/config'), api('/api/config/ai')]);
    const c = config;
    document.getElementById('settingsLoading').style.display = 'none';
    document.getElementById('settingsForm').style.display = 'block';

    // SSH
    setVal('cfg-ssh-host', c.ssh.host);
    setVal('cfg-ssh-port', c.ssh.port);
    setVal('cfg-ssh-user', c.ssh.user);
    setVal('cfg-ssh-key_path', c.ssh.key_path);
    setVal('cfg-ssh-base_path', c.ssh.base_path);
    setVal('cfg-ssh-filename_prefix_length', c.ssh.filename_prefix_length);

    // Clipboard
    setVal('cfg-clipboard-min_length', c.clipboard.min_length);
    setVal('cfg-clipboard-max_length', c.clipboard.max_length);
    setVal('cfg-clipboard-poll_interval_ms', c.clipboard.poll_interval_ms);
    setVal('cfg-clipboard-exclude_words', (c.clipboard.exclude_words || []).join(', '));

    // Sync
    setChecked('cfg-sync-enabled', c.sync.enabled);
    setVal('cfg-sync-max_retries', c.sync.max_retries);
    setVal('cfg-sync-retry_delay_ms', c.sync.retry_delay_ms);

    // Web
    setVal('cfg-web-port', c.web.port);
    setVal('cfg-web-auth', ''); // always empty for security
    setVal('cfg-web-refresh_sec', c.web.refresh_sec || '');
    setVal('cfg-web-log_refresh_sec', c.web.log_refresh_sec || '');

    // Relay
    setChecked('cfg-relay-enabled', c.relay.enabled);
    setVal('cfg-relay-endpoint', c.relay.endpoint);
    setVal('cfg-relay-secret', '');
    setVal('cfg-relay-pull_interval_sec', c.relay.pull_interval_sec);

    // Blog
    setChecked('cfg-blog-enabled', c.blog.enabled);
    setVal('cfg-blog-api_url', c.blog.api_url);
    setVal('cfg-blog-tags', c.blog.tags);

    // Podcast
    setChecked('cfg-podcast-enabled', c.podcast.enabled);
    setVal('cfg-podcast-api_url', c.podcast.api_url);
    setVal('cfg-podcast-app_id', c.podcast.app_id);

    // IMA
    setChecked('cfg-ima-enabled', c.ima.enabled);
    setVal('cfg-ima-api_url', c.ima.api_url);
    setVal('cfg-ima-client_id', c.ima.client_id);
    setVal('cfg-ima-api_key', '');
    setVal('cfg-ima-folder_id', c.ima.folder_id);

    // Kindle
    setChecked('cfg-kindle-enabled', c.kindle.enabled);
    setVal('cfg-kindle-sender_email', c.kindle.sender_email);
    setVal('cfg-kindle-sender_password', '');
    setVal('cfg-kindle-smtp_server', c.kindle.smtp_server);
    setVal('cfg-kindle-smtp_port', c.kindle.smtp_port);
    setVal('cfg-kindle-kindle_email', c.kindle.kindle_email);

    // AI (from dedicated endpoint which includes presets/templates)
    const ai = aiData.config;
    setChecked('cfg-ai-enabled', ai.enabled);
    setVal('cfg-ai-endpoint', ai.endpoint);
    setVal('cfg-ai-api_key', '');
    setVal('cfg-ai-model', ai.model);
    setVal('cfg-ai-prompt', ai.prompt || '');
    setVal('cfg-ai-min_content_len', ai.min_content_len);
    setVal('cfg-ai-max_content_len', ai.max_content_len);
    setVal('cfg-ai-timeout_sec', ai.timeout_sec);

    // AI preset dropdown
    const presetSel = document.getElementById('cfg-ai-preset');
    presetSel.innerHTML = '<option value="custom">自定义</option>';
    if (aiData.presets) {
      for (const [key, val] of Object.entries(aiData.presets)) {
        const opt = document.createElement('option');
        opt.value = key;
        opt.textContent = val.label || key;
        if (ai.preset === key) opt.selected = true;
        presetSel.appendChild(opt);
      }
    }
    presetSel.onchange = function() {
      const p = aiData.presets && aiData.presets[this.value];
      if (p) {
        document.getElementById('cfg-ai-endpoint').value = p.endpoint;
        document.getElementById('cfg-ai-model').value = p.model;
      }
    };
    setVal('cfg-ai-preset', ai.preset || 'custom');

    // AI prompt template dropdown
    const tmplSel = document.getElementById('cfg-ai-prompt_template');
    tmplSel.innerHTML = '<option value="">通用模式（默认）</option>';
    if (aiData.prompt_templates) {
      for (const [key, val] of Object.entries(aiData.prompt_templates)) {
        const opt = document.createElement('option');
        opt.value = val;
        opt.textContent = key;
        tmplSel.appendChild(opt);
      }
    }
    tmplSel.onchange = function() {
      if (this.value) document.getElementById('cfg-ai-prompt').value = this.value;
    };
    // Restore template selection
    if (ai.prompt_template) {
      const tmplOpts = tmplSel.options;
      for (let i = 0; i < tmplOpts.length; i++) {
        if (tmplOpts[i].textContent === ai.prompt_template) { tmplOpts[i].selected = true; break; }
      }
    }
  } catch (e) {}
}

async function saveAllConfig() {
  const excludeWords = document.getElementById('cfg-clipboard-exclude_words').value
    .split(',').map(s => s.trim()).filter(Boolean);
  const body = {
    ssh: {
      host: getVal('cfg-ssh-host'), port: getVal('cfg-ssh-port'), user: getVal('cfg-ssh-user'),
      key_path: getVal('cfg-ssh-key_path'), base_path: getVal('cfg-ssh-base_path'),
      filename_prefix_length: getInt('cfg-ssh-filename_prefix_length')
    },
    clipboard: {
      min_length: getInt('cfg-clipboard-min_length'), max_length: getInt('cfg-clipboard-max_length'),
      poll_interval_ms: getInt('cfg-clipboard-poll_interval_ms'), exclude_words: excludeWords
    },
    sync: {
      enabled: getChecked('cfg-sync-enabled'), max_retries: getInt('cfg-sync-max_retries'),
      retry_delay_ms: getInt('cfg-sync-retry_delay_ms')
    },
    web: { enabled: true, port: getInt('cfg-web-port'), auth: getVal('cfg-web-auth'), refresh_sec: getInt('cfg-web-refresh_sec'), log_refresh_sec: getInt('cfg-web-log_refresh_sec') },
    relay: {
      enabled: getChecked('cfg-relay-enabled'), endpoint: getVal('cfg-relay-endpoint'),
      secret: getVal('cfg-relay-secret'), pull_interval_sec: getInt('cfg-relay-pull_interval_sec')
    },
    blog: { enabled: getChecked('cfg-blog-enabled'), api_url: getVal('cfg-blog-api_url'), tags: getVal('cfg-blog-tags') },
    podcast: { enabled: getChecked('cfg-podcast-enabled'), api_url: getVal('cfg-podcast-api_url'), app_id: getVal('cfg-podcast-app_id') },
    ima: {
      enabled: getChecked('cfg-ima-enabled'), api_url: getVal('cfg-ima-api_url'),
      client_id: getVal('cfg-ima-client_id'), api_key: getVal('cfg-ima-api_key'), folder_id: getVal('cfg-ima-folder_id')
    },
    kindle: {
      enabled: getChecked('cfg-kindle-enabled'), sender_email: getVal('cfg-kindle-sender_email'),
      sender_password: getVal('cfg-kindle-sender_password'), smtp_server: getVal('cfg-kindle-smtp_server'),
      smtp_port: getInt('cfg-kindle-smtp_port'), kindle_email: getVal('cfg-kindle-kindle_email')
    },
    ai: {
      enabled: getChecked('cfg-ai-enabled'), preset: getVal('cfg-ai-preset'),
      endpoint: getVal('cfg-ai-endpoint'), api_key: getVal('cfg-ai-api_key'),
      model: getVal('cfg-ai-model'), prompt: getVal('cfg-ai-prompt'),
      prompt_template: document.getElementById('cfg-ai-prompt_template').selectedOptions[0]?.textContent || '',
      min_content_len: getInt('cfg-ai-min_content_len'), max_content_len: getInt('cfg-ai-max_content_len'),
      timeout_sec: getInt('cfg-ai-timeout_sec')
    }
  };
  try {
    const res = await fetch('/api/config', {
      method: 'PUT', headers: {'Content-Type': 'application/json'}, body: JSON.stringify(body)
    });
    const data = await res.json();
    if (data.error) { showToast('保存失败: ' + data.error); }
    else { showToast('设置已保存'); loadAllConfig(); }
  } catch (e) { showToast('保存失败: ' + e.message); }
}

function setVal(id, val) { const el = document.getElementById(id); if (el) el.value = val ?? ''; }
function getVal(id) { const el = document.getElementById(id); return el ? el.value : ''; }
function getInt(id) { const el = document.getElementById(id); return el ? parseInt(el.value) || 0 : 0; }
function setChecked(id, val) { const el = document.getElementById(id); if (el) el.checked = !!val; }
function getChecked(id) { const el = document.getElementById(id); return el ? el.checked : false; }

function updateUptime() {
  if (!adminStatus || adminStatus._fetchedAt === undefined) return;
  const sec = adminStatus.uptime + Math.floor((Date.now() - adminStatus._fetchedAt) / 1000);
  const d = Math.floor(sec / 86400);
  const h = Math.floor((sec % 86400) / 3600);
  const m = Math.floor((sec % 3600) / 60);
  const s = sec % 60;
  let str = '';
  if (d > 0) str += d + ' 天 ';
  str += h + ' 小时 ' + m + ' 分钟 ' + s + ' 秒';
  document.getElementById('adminUptime').textContent = str;
}

async function restartKnowly() {
  if (!confirm('确定要重启 Knowly 吗？')) return;
  try {
    await fetch('/api/admin/restart', { method: 'POST' });
    showToast('正在重启，等待服务就绪...');
    setTimeout(() => { reloadWhenReady(); }, 3000);
  } catch (e) {
    showToast('重启请求已发送，等待服务就绪...');
    setTimeout(() => { reloadWhenReady(); }, 3000);
  }
}

async function updateKnowly() {
  if (!confirm('确定要从源码编译并更新吗？')) return;
  const btn = document.getElementById('updateBtn');
  btn.disabled = true;
  btn.textContent = '更新中...';
  try {
    const resp = await fetch('/api/admin/update', { method: 'POST' });
    const reader = resp.body.getReader();
    const decoder = new TextDecoder();
    let done = false;
    while (!done) {
      const { value, done: d } = await reader.read();
      done = d;
      if (value) {
        const text = decoder.decode(value);
        text.split('\n').forEach(line => {
          if (line.startsWith('data: ')) {
            try {
              const ev = JSON.parse(line.slice(6));
              btn.textContent = ev.message;
              if (ev.step === 'error') {
                showToast(ev.message);
                btn.disabled = false;
                btn.textContent = '更新';
              }
              if (ev.step === 'done') {
                showToast('更新完成，等待服务就绪...');
                setTimeout(() => { reloadWhenReady(); }, 2000);
              }
            } catch(e) {}
          }
        });
      }
    }
  } catch (e) {
    showToast('更新请求已发送，等待服务就绪...');
    setTimeout(() => { reloadWhenReady(); }, 3000);
  }
}

function reloadWhenReady() {
  fetch('/api/status', { cache: 'no-store' }).then(r => {
    if (r.ok) location.reload();
    else throw new Error();
  }).catch(() => {
    setTimeout(() => { reloadWhenReady(); }, 2000);
  });
}

async function releaseKnowly() {
  if (!confirm('确定要发布新版本吗？（git push → npm version minor → git push --tags）')) return;
  const btn = document.getElementById('releaseBtn');
  btn.disabled = true;
  btn.textContent = '发布中...';
  try {
    const resp = await fetch('/api/admin/release', { method: 'POST' });
    const reader = resp.body.getReader();
    const decoder = new TextDecoder();
    let done = false;
    while (!done) {
      const { value, done: d } = await reader.read();
      done = d;
      if (value) {
        const text = decoder.decode(value);
        text.split('\n').forEach(line => {
          if (line.startsWith('data: ')) {
            try {
              const ev = JSON.parse(line.slice(6));
              btn.textContent = ev.message;
              if (ev.step === 'error') {
                showToast(ev.message);
                btn.disabled = false;
                btn.textContent = '发布';
              }
              if (ev.step === 'done') {
                showToast(ev.message);
                btn.disabled = false;
                btn.textContent = '发布';
              }
            } catch(e) {}
          }
        });
      }
    }
  } catch (e) {
    showToast('发布失败');
    btn.disabled = false;
    btn.textContent = '发布';
  }
}

// === Util ===
function escHtml(s) {
  const d = document.createElement('div');
  d.textContent = s;
  return d.innerHTML;
}
function escAttr(s) {
  return JSON.stringify(s).replace(/'/g, "\\'");
}

// === Theme ===
function setTheme(t) {
  if (t === 'default') document.documentElement.removeAttribute('data-theme');
  else document.documentElement.setAttribute('data-theme', t);
  localStorage.setItem('knowly-theme', t);
  document.querySelectorAll('.theme-option').forEach(o => o.classList.toggle('active', o.dataset.theme === t));
  document.getElementById('themeDropdown').classList.remove('show');
}
function toggleThemeMenu() {
  document.getElementById('themeDropdown').classList.toggle('show');
}
(function() {
  var t = localStorage.getItem('knowly-theme') || 'default';
  if (t !== 'default') document.documentElement.setAttribute('data-theme', t);
  document.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
    if (!e.target.closest('.header-left')) {
      document.getElementById('themeDropdown').classList.remove('show');
    }
  });
})();

// === Init ===
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
  showMotto();
  loadLogs();
  connectLogStream();
  loadStatus();
  setInterval(loadStatus, (LOG_REFRESH_SEC || 30) * 1000);

  // 标签栏点击事件委托
  document.getElementById('tagsBar').addEventListener('click', function(e) {
    var el = e.target.closest('.tag-item');
    if (!el) return;
    filterByTag(el.dataset.tag || '');
  });

  // 日志行点击复制
  document.getElementById('logContainer').addEventListener('click', function(e) {
    var line = e.target.closest('.log-line');
    if (line) {
      var text = line.dataset.raw || line.querySelector('.log-msg').textContent;
      copyText(text);
    }
  });
});
</script>
</body>
</html>
````
